360/5 * 3).\n       *                                For a 7 pointed star, we might do\n       *                                360/7 * 3 = 154.286)\n       *      SHRINK_TIME = 400ms\n       */\n\n      :host {\n        display: inline-block;\n        position: relative;\n        width: 28px;\n        height: 28px;\n\n        /* 360 * ARCTIME / (ARCSTARTROT + (360-ARCSIZE)) */\n        --paper-spinner-container-rotation-duration: 1568ms;\n\n        /* ARCTIME */\n        --paper-spinner-expand-contract-duration: 1333ms;\n\n        /* 4 * ARCTIME */\n
